#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
# Termux → Repo Sync (SSH Auto)

# 3️⃣ Start ssh-agent

Pulling latest..." | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";     git -C "$REPO_DIR" pull --rebase 2>&1 | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log" || {         echo "[X] Pull failed!" | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";         exit 1;     }; else     echo "[✓] Cloning repo..." | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";     git clone "$REPO_URL" "$REPO_DIR" 2>&1 | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log" || {         echo "[X] Clone failed!" | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";         exit 1;     }; fi

#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
# find-all-html-files.sh - COMPREHENSIVE HTML FILE SEARCH
echo -e "${BLUE}║  Total Recall - All Locations              ║${NC}"
# 7. Total Recall Files
echo -e "${YELLOW}[7/12] Total Recall Files...${NC}"
RECALL_LOCATIONS=(     "$HOME/total-recall"     "$HOME/totalrecall"     "$HOME/recall"     "$HOME/.recall"     "$HOME/memory"     "$HOME/.memory"     "$HOME/archive"     "$HOME/.archive" )
for loc in "${RECALL_LOCATIONS[@]}"; do     if [ -d "$loc" ]; then         find "$loc" -type f \( -name "*.html" -o -name "*.htm" \) 2>/dev/null | while read -r file; do             size=$(stat -f%z "$file" 2>/dev/null || stat -c%s "$file" 2>/dev/null || echo 0);             echo "$file|$size|recall" >> "$MASTER_LIST";         done;     fi; done
count=$(grep -c "recall" "$MASTER_LIST" 2>/dev/null || echo 0)
# 9. Constellation25 & Agentik

# Agent 1: Discovery — find candidate directories

echo "🤖 [File Hunter Agent] Scanning for agent-like files (depth $MAX_DEPTH)..."
find $TARGET_DIRS -maxdepth $MAX_DEPTH -type f   \( -iname "*.js" -o -iname "*.sh" -o -iname "*.py" \)   -not -path "*/$IGNORE_PATTERNS/*"   -not -path "*/.git/*"   2>/dev/null | grep -iE "$AGENT_PATTERNS" | sort | tee \~/c25-found-files.txt
echo "📊 Found $(wc -l < \~/c25-found-files.txt) candidate files. Saved to \~/c25-found-files.txt"
# Agent 3: Repo Inspector — quick git remote / status per repo dir
echo "🤖 [Repo Inspector Agent] Checking git repos under \~/github-repos..."
find \~/github-repos -maxdepth 4 -type d -name ".git" 2>/dev/null | while read gitdir; do   repodir=$(dirname "$gitdir");   cd "$repodir" || continue;   remote=$(git remote -v | head -1 | awk '{print $2}' || echo "no remote");   branch=$(git branch --show-current 2>/dev/null || echo "detached");   echo "Repo: $repodir";   echo "  Remote: $remote";   echo "  Branch: $branch";   echo ""; done | head -40   # Limit output flood
echo "--- .constellation25 contents (likely gold) ---"
ls -la \~/.constellation25 2>/dev/null || echo "Not found"
echo "--- Agents subdir ---"
ls -la \~/.constellation25/agents 2>/dev/null | head -20
ls -la \~/.constellation25/modules \~/.constellation25/config 2>/dev/null
echo "--- .agent-engine (runtime?) ---"
ls -la \~/.agent-engine 2>/dev/null
echo "--- .c25 keys/parse ---"
ls -la \~/.c25 2>/dev/null

#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
# C25 REAL STACK LAUNCHER
# Wires your existing services + agents into one system
SOVEREIGN_GTP="$HOME/github-repos/Constillation25/sovereign_gtp"
AGENTS_DIR="$SOVEREIGN_GTP/agents"
BACKEND="$SOVEREIGN_GTP/backend"
MYBUYO_BIOMETRIC="$HOME/github-repos/FacePrintPay/mybuyo-biometric-saas"
DIGITAL_DOLLAR="$HOME/github-repos/FacePrintPay/digital-dollar"
PATHOS="$HOME/pathos"
CONSTELLATION25="$HOME/constellation-25"
AGENT_LOGS="$HOME/agent_logs"
mkdir -p "$AGENT_LOGS"
log()   { echo "[$(stamp)] $*" | tee -a "$LOGS/c25-real.log"; }
log "║  C25 REAL STACK — GREENSBORO LAUNCH  ║"
log "Agents: $(ls $AGENTS_DIR/*.sh 2>/dev/null | wc -l) bash agents found"
# PaTHos / Sovereign GTP Backend — port 3000 + WS 8080
if port_up 3000; then   log "✓  PaTHos/Backend :3000 already running"; else   log "   Starting PaTHos backend...";   kill_port 3000;   cd "$BACKEND" && nohup node server.js >> "$LOGS/pathos.log" 2>&1 &   wait_port 3000 "PaTHos"; fi
if port_up 3005; then   log "✓  Digital Dollar :3005 already running"; else   log "   Starting Digital Dollar...";   kill_port 3005;   cd "$DIGITAL_DOLLAR" && nohup node api/server.js >> "$LOGS/digital-dollar.log" 2>&1 &   wait_port 3005 "DigitalDollar"; fi
if port_up 3001; then   log "✓  MyBuyo Dashboard :3001 already running"; else   log "   Starting MyBuyo Dashboard...";   kill_port 3001;   cd "$MYBUYO_RESTORE/services/dashboard" && nohup node index.js >> "$LOGS/mybuyo-dashboard.log" 2>&1 &   wait_port 3001 "MyBuyo-Dashboard"; fi
if port_up 3003; then   log "✓  MyBuyo Swarm :3003 already running"; else   log "   Starting MyBuyo Swarm API...";   kill_port 3003;   cd "$MYBUYO_RESTORE/services/swarm_api" && nohup node index.js >> "$LOGS/mybuyo-swarm.log" 2>&1 &   wait_port 3003 "MyBuyo-Swarm"; fi
if port_up 3004; then   log "✓  MyBuyo Biometric :3004 already running"; else   log "   Starting MyBuyo Biometric...";   kill_port 3004;   cd "$MYBUYO_BIOMETRIC" && nohup node server.js >> "$LOGS/mybuyo-biometric.log" 2>&1 &   wait_port 3004 "MyBuyo-Biometric"; fi
# ── PHASE 2: Constellation-25 server ─────────────────────────
log "PHASE 2 :: Constellation-25"
if [ -f "$CONSTELLATION25/server.js" ]; then   if port_up 4000; then     log "✓  C25 server already running";   else     log "   Starting Constellation-25 server...";     cd "$CONSTELLATION25" && nohup node server.js >> "$LOGS/constellation25.log" 2>&1 &     sleep 3;     port_up 4000 && log "✓  C25 :4000 ONLINE" || log "   C25 server started (port TBD)";   fi; else   log "   C25 server.js found at: $(find $CONSTELLATION25 -name 'server.js' 2>/dev/null | head -1)"; fi
# ── PHASE 3: Spawn existing bash agents ──────────────────────
log "PHASE 3 :: Spawning Constellation Agents"
# Kill old agent instances cleanly
pkill -f "persistent-agents" 2>/dev/null
# Spawn each real agent script
AGENT_COUNT=0
for agent_script in "$AGENTS_DIR"/*.sh; do   [ -f "$agent_script" ] || continue;   agent_name=$(basename "$agent_script" .sh);
if pgrep -f "$agent_script" > /dev/null 2>&1; then     log "✓  $agent_name already running";   else     nohup bash "$agent_script" >> "$AGENT_LOGS/${agent_name}.log" 2>&1 &     log "   Spawned: $agent_name (PID $!)";   fi;   AGENT_COUNT=$((AGENT_COUNT+1));   sleep 0.3; done
log "   $AGENT_COUNT agents spawned from $AGENTS_DIR"
# Also run the persistent agent system if it exists
if [ -f "$HOME/c25-persistent-agents.sh" ]; then   pgrep -f "c25-persistent-agents" > /dev/null || {     log "   Starting c25-persistent-agents...";     nohup bash "$HOME/c25-persistent-agents.sh" >> "$AGENT_LOGS/persistent.log" 2>&1 &     log "   Persistent agent system PID: $!";   }; fi
# ── PHASE 4: Wire agents to services via MCP calls ───────────
log "PHASE 4 :: Registering agents with PaTHos MCP"
register_agent() {   local name=$1 port=$2 role=$3;   curl -s -X POST http://localhost:3000/agent/register     -H "Content-Type: application/json"     -d "{\"agent\":\"$name\",\"port\":$port,\"role\":\"$role\",\"ts\":\"$(date -u +%Y-%m-%dT%H:%M:%SZ)\"}"     2>/dev/null | grep -q "ok" && log "   Registered: $name" || log "   Skipped: $name (MCP not ready)"; }
# Register confirmed running services as agents
register_agent "PaTHos"    3000 "SovereignMind"
register_agent "DD-Dollar" 3005 "Revenue"
register_agent "MyBuyo"    3001 "Identity"
register_agent "Biometric" 3004 "Auth"
register_agent "SwarmAPI"  3003 "Orchestrator"
# Register each bash agent
for agent_script in "$AGENTS_DIR"/*.sh; do   [ -f "$agent_script" ] || continue;   agent_name=$(basename "$agent_script" .sh);   register_agent "$agent_name" 0 "BashAgent"; done
log "║  C25 STACK STATUS                    ║"
for entry in   "3000:PaTHos/Backend"   "3001:MyBuyo-Dashboard"   "3003:MyBuyo-Swarm"   "3004:MyBuyo-Biometric"   "3005:Digital-Dollar"   "8080:WebSocket"; do   port="${entry%%:*}";   name="${entry##*:}";   if port_up $port; then     log "  🟢 $name :$port";   else     log "  🔴 $name :$port";   fi; done
log "  Agents running: $(pgrep -f 'agents/' | wc -l)"
log "  Node procs:     $(pgrep -c node 2>/dev/null || echo 0)"
log "  Verify PaTHos:  curl http://localhost:3000"
log "  DD\$:           curl http://localhost:3005"
log "  Logs:           tail -f $LOGS/c25-real.log"
pkg install tar gzip ncompress   # ncompress provides compress/uncompress
zcat project.tar.z | tar -xvf -   # extract everything here
zcat project.tar.z | tar -xvf - -C ./extracted-folder

A **sovereign, human‑gated pipeline** that cleanly separates **intent**, **execution**, and **authority**.

#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
# C25 AGENT READINESS — Make all files runnable by agents
# Operator: u0_a510 | TotalRecall anchored
C25_HOME="$HOME/constellation25"
LOG="$C25_HOME/logs/agent_readiness.log"
MANIFEST="$C25_HOME/logs/totalrecall_manifest.log"
mkdir -p "$C25_HOME/logs"
echo "  ║     C25 AGENT READINESS — FULL REPO WIRING          ║"
# ── STANDARD run.sh TEMPLATE ─────────────────────────────────
# Every repo that lacks a run.sh gets this injected
#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
# C25 AGENT RUNNER — $repo_name
# Auto-generated by c25-agent-readiness.sh
C25_HOME="\$HOME/constellation25"
LOG="\$C25_HOME/logs/\$REPO_NAME.log"
MANIFEST="\$C25_HOME/logs/totalrecall_manifest.log"
mkdir -p "\$C25_HOME/logs"
echo "[\$(ts)] [C25] [\$REPO_NAME] AGENT START" | tee -a "\$LOG"
node "\$(dirname \$0)/index.js" "\$@"
python3 "\$(dirname \$0)/main.py" "\$@"
node "\$(dirname \$0)/src/index.js" "\$@"
python3 "\$(dirname \$0)/src/main.py" "\$@"
echo "[\$(ts)] [C25] [\$REPO_NAME] AGENT DONE" | tee -a "\$LOG"
chmod +x "$repo_path/run.sh"; }

agent_json+="]"
log DONE "Stage 3 — 25 agents complete"
echo "$agent_json"

local artifact="$C25_HOME/gamma-artifact.html"

el.innerHTML='<div class="an">'+a.agent.toUpperCase()+'</div><div class="ar">'+a.role+'</div><div style="font-size:9px;color:var(--green);margin-bottom:4px;">'+a.status+'</div><div style="font-size:8px;color:rgba(0,255,136,.35)">'+a.sha.substring(0,16)+'...</div>';

#!/usr/bin/env bash
# CONSTELLATION 25 - ULTIMATE PLANETARY SWARM v5.0
# Powered by Pathos-Sovereign-1
CONFIG_DIR="$HOME/.constellation25"
REPORT="$HOME/CONSTELLATION25_SWARM_REPORT.html"
REPOS=("digital-dollar" "videocourts" "constellation25")
MAGENTA='\033[0;35m'
agent() {   local agent_name="$1";   local status="$2";   log "${CYAN}🌌 [AGENT: $agent_name]${NC} $status"; }
banner() {   clear;   echo -e "${BLUE}╔════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╗${NC}";   echo -e "${BLUE}║${NC}          ${CYAN}CONSTELLATION 25 - ULTIMATE SWARM v5.0${NC}          ${BLUE}║${NC}";   echo -e "${BLUE}║${NC}               ${GREEN}Pathos-Sovereign-1 Core${NC}                   ${BLUE}║${NC}";   echo -e "${BLUE}║${NC}        ${MAGENTA}Visual Interface + Real API Integration${NC}        ${BLUE}║${NC}";   echo -e "${BLUE}╚════════════════════════════════════════════════════════════╝${NC}";   echo ""; }
if [ ! -f "$CLAUDE_API_KEY_FILE" ]; then     warning "Claude API key not found";     echo -e "${YELLOW}Enter your Claude API key (from console.anthropic.com):${NC}";     read -r api_key;     if [ -n "$api_key" ]; then       echo "$api_key" > "$CLAUDE_API_KEY_FILE";       chmod 600 "$CLAUDE_API_KEY_FILE";       success "Claude API key saved";     fi;   fi;
if [ ! -f "$GITHUB_TOKEN_FILE" ]; then     warning "GitHub token not found";     echo -e "${YELLOW}Enter your GitHub token (optional, press Enter to skip):${NC}";     read -r gh_token;     if [ -n "$gh_token" ]; then       echo "$gh_token" > "$GITHUB_TOKEN_FILE";       chmod 600 "$GITHUB_TOKEN_FILE";       success "GitHub token saved";     fi;   fi;      CLAUDE_API_KEY=$(cat "$CLAUDE_API_KEY_FILE" 2>/dev/null || echo "");   GITHUB_TOKEN=$(cat "$GITHUB_TOKEN_FILE" 2>/dev/null || echo ""); }
# --- Agent Roster (25 Specialized Agents) ---
AGENT_NAMES=(   "Scaffold" "Compile" "Parse" "Prune" "Configure"   "Debug" "Package" "Deploy" "Secure" "Monitor"   "Optimize" "Test" "Validate" "Integrate" "Release"   "Backup" "Restore" "Scale" "Balance" "Encrypt"   "Decrypt" "Network" "Storage" "Compute" "Govern" )
# --- Termux API Agents ---
agent_termux_battery() {   agent "Termux::Battery" "Reading device battery status...";   sleep 0.2;      if command -v termux-battery-status &> /dev/null; then     local battery_json=$(termux-battery-status 2>/dev/null);     if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then       local battery_level=$(echo "$battery_json" | grep -o '"percentage":[0-9]*' | grep -o '[0-9]*' || echo "0");       success "Battery: ${battery_level}% | Data cached";       echo "$battery_json" > "$API_CACHE/battery.json";       return 0;     fi;   fi;      warning "Termux API not available (install: pkg install termux-api)";   return 1; }
agent_termux_wifi() {   agent "Termux::WiFi" "Scanning WiFi networks...";   sleep 0.2;      if command -v termux-wifi-scaninfo &> /dev/null; then     local wifi=$(termux-wifi-scaninfo 2>/dev/null);     if [ $? -eq 0 ]; then       success "WiFi scan complete | Networks detected";       echo "$wifi" > "$API_CACHE/wifi.json";       return 0;     fi;   fi;      warning "WiFi scan unavailable";   return 1; }
agent_termux_notification() {   agent "Termux::Notify" "Sending system notification...";   sleep 0.1;      if command -v termux-notification &> /dev/null; then     termux-notification --title "Constellation 25" --content "Swarm deployment initiated" 2>/dev/null;     success "Notification delivered";     return 0;   fi;      warning "Notifications unavailable";   return 1; }
agent_termux_location() {   agent "Termux::Location" "Acquiring GPS coordinates...";   sleep 0.2;      if command -v termux-location &> /dev/null; then     timeout 3 termux-location -p network > "$API_CACHE/location.json" 2>/dev/null &&       success "GPS location acquired" || warning "Location timeout";   else     warning "Location API unavailable";   fi; }

# --- GitHub API Agents ---
agent_github_status() {   agent "GitHub::Status" "Checking GitHub API status...";   sleep 0.2;      local status=$(curl -s https://www.githubstatus.com/api/v2/status.json 2>/dev/null);   if echo "$status" | grep -q "operational"; then     success "GitHub API operational";     return 0;   else     warning "GitHub may be experiencing issues";     return 1;   fi; }
agent_github_repos() {   agent "GitHub::Repos" "Scanning local repositories...";   sleep 0.3;      local tracked=0;   local total=${#REPOS[@]};      for repo in "${REPOS[@]}"; do     local repo_path="$REPOS_DIR/$repo";          if [ -d "$repo_path/.git" ]; then       cd "$repo_path";       if git remote get-url origin &>/dev/null; then         success "✓ $repo (tracked with remote)";         tracked=$((tracked + 1));       else         warning "✗ $repo (no remote configured)";       fi;     else       warning "✗ $repo (not a git repository)";     fi;   done;      success "Repository sync: $tracked/$total tracked"; }
# --- FileSystem Agent ---
agent_filesystem_scan() {   agent "FileSystem::Scan" "Analyzing project structure...";   sleep 0.3;      local total_files=0;   local total_dirs=0;      for repo in "${REPOS[@]}"; do     if [ -d "$REPOS_DIR/$repo" ]; then       local files=$(find "$REPOS_DIR/$repo" -type f 2>/dev/null | wc -l);       local dirs=$(find "$REPOS_DIR/$repo" -type d 2>/dev/null | wc -l);       local size=$(du -sh "$REPOS_DIR/$repo" 2>/dev/null | cut -f1);              total_files=$((total_files + files));       total_dirs=$((total_dirs + dirs));              log "  ${BLUE}└─${NC} $repo: $files files, $dirs dirs, $size";     fi;   done;      success "Scanned $total_files files in $total_dirs directories"; }
# --- Build Agent ---

main() {   if [ ! -d "$CONFIG_DIR" ]; then     warning "Configuration directory missing. Creating...";     mkdir -p "$CONFIG_DIR";   fi;    try_count=0;   max_tries=3;      while [ $try_count -lt $max_tries ]; do     set +e;     run_ultimate_swarm;     exit_code=$?;     set -e;          if [ $exit_code -eq 0 ]; then       break;     else       try_count=$((try_count + 1));       error "Swarm interruption detected. Retry $try_count/$max_tries";       agent "Govern" "Initiating recovery protocol...";       sleep 2;     fi;   done;    echo "";   echo -e "${GREEN}✅ SYSTEM READY. ALL AGENTS OPERATIONAL.${NC}";   echo -e "${CYAN}Check $REPORT for full deployment details.${NC}"; }

# Find all .sh files in vault and home
bin/bash
# Sync agent hierarchy across all C25 agents
AGENT_DIRS=(     ~/.agent-engine     ~/.agent_locks     ~/.agent_pids     ~/.agent_temp     ~/.c25     ~/.c25parse     ~/.constellation25     ~/.total_recall     ~/agent_logs     ~/agents     ~/logs     ~/output     ~/tasks )

#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
REPO_SSH="git@github.com:FacePrintPay/your-repo.git"
REPO_NAME=$(basename -s .git "$REPO_SSH")
LOG_DIR="$HOME/YesQuidLogs"
# Ensure Git is installed
if ! command -v git &>/dev/null; then     echo "[!] Git not found, installing..." | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";     pkg install -y git | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log"; fi
# Ensure SSH agent is running
if ! pgrep -x "ssh-agent" > /dev/null; then     echo "[*] Starting ssh-agent..." | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";     eval $(ssh-agent -s) | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";     ssh-add ~/.ssh/id_ed25519 | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log"; fi
if [ -d "$REPO_DIR/.git" ]; then     echo "[✓] Repo exists. Pulling latest..." | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";     git -C "$REPO_DIR" pull --rebase 2>&1 | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log" || {         echo "[X] Pull failed!" | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";         exit 1;     }; else     echo "[✓] Cloning repo..." | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";     git clone "$REPO_SSH" "$REPO_DIR" 2>&1 | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log" || {         echo "[X] Clone failed!" | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";         exit 1;     }; fi
#!/data/data/com.termux/files/usr/bin/bash
# Termux → Repo Sync (SSH Auto)
REPO_URL="git@github.com:FacePrintPay/your-repo.git"
REPO_NAME=$(basename -s .git "$REPO_URL")
LOG_DIR="$HOME/YesQuidLogs"
# 1️⃣ Ensure Git is installed
if ! command -v git &>/dev/null; then     echo "[!] Git not found, installing..." | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";     pkg install -y git | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log"; fi
# 2️⃣ Ensure SSH key exists
if [ ! -f "$HOME/.ssh/id_ed25519" ]; then     echo "[*] SSH key not found. Generating..." | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";     ssh-keygen -t ed25519 -C "your_email@example.com" -f "$HOME/.ssh/id_ed25519" -N ""; fi
# 3️⃣ Start ssh-agent
eval $(ssh-agent -s) | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log"
if [ -d "$REPO_DIR/.git" ]; then     echo "[✓] Repo exists. Pulling latest..." | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";     git -C "$REPO_DIR" pull --rebase 2>&1 | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log" || {         echo "[X] Pull failed!" | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";         exit 1;     }; else     echo "[✓] Cloning repo..." | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";     git clone "$REPO_URL" "$REPO_DIR" 2>&1 | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log" || {         echo "[X] Clone failed!" | tee -a "$LOG_DIR/repo_sync.log";         exit 1;     }; fi
